msg:Located in the High-tech Zone, about 10 kilometers to the old town. We didn't order breakfast, so we had to drive 30 minutes to have morning tea in the morning. There is only Tianhong next to it, and it is about seven kilometers away from Mixc, which is quite lively. The room is large, and the bed is 2 meters long, so it is no problem for our family of three to sleep. The bathroom is separated into three parts, with a bathtub and a washlet. The air conditioning has almost no cooling effect, but fortunately the temperature is not high, about 20 degrees, and I slept without a quilt. The swimming pool is on the fifth floor, open from 9 to 21, and slippers are not allowed. The children wore their own shoes and brought a pair of slippers. The water temperature was a little cool, because it was the last morning of the long holiday, so we reserved the place. A 15-yuan small supermarket voucher was given on the first day of the stay, but not on the second day. Overall, it's not bad, except that the location is a bit remote
